    function addtocart(pid){
      var beforeCookieValue = getCookie(cookieName="dest_area",cookieValue=null);
      layer.open({
          type: 2,
          content: encodeURI('//product.dangdang.com?r=combo/index&productId='+pid+'&source=搜索'),
          area:['870px','430px'],
          cancel: function(index, layero){  
              // if(confirm('确定要关闭么')){ //只有当点击confirm框的确定时，该层才会关闭
                  layer.close(index);
                  var afterCookieValue = getCookie(afterCookieName="dest_area",cookieValue=null);
                  if(afterCookieValue != beforeCookieValue){
                     window.location.reload();
                  }
              //}
              return false;
          }
      });  
    }
    function getCookie(cookieName,cookieValue){
       if (document.cookie && document.cookie != '') { 
          var cookies = document.cookie.split(';');
          for (var i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) { 
              var cookie = cookies[i];
              if (cookie.substring(0, cookieName.length + 2).trim() == cookieName.trim() + "=") {
                cookieValue = cookie.substring(cookieName.length + 2, cookie.length);
                var arr = cookieValue.match(/province_id(\S*)city_id/);;
                cookieValue= arr[1];
                break 
              } 
          } 
      }
      return cookieValue;
    }

        $(window).scroll(function(e){
                var top = $(".classify_nav").offset().top+$(".classify_nav").height()-2; 
                var scrolltop = $(document).scrollTop();
                if(scrolltop >= top){
                    $(".submenu").show();
                }else{
                    $(".submenu").hide();
                }
                var now = $(".submenu").find(".now").parents('li').attr('id');
                var next = $(".submenu").find(".now").parents('li').next('li').attr('id');
                var prev = $(".submenu").find(".now").parents('li').prev('li').attr('id');
                var floor_top = 0;
                var floor_top_next = 0;
                var floor_top_prev = 0;
                if(now != undefined){
                    now_floor = now.replace('navfloat','floor');
                    floor_top = $("#"+now_floor).offset().top;
                    now_nav = now.replace('navfloat','nav');
                    if(next != undefined){
                         next_floor = next.replace('navfloat','floor');
                         floor_top_next = $("#"+next_floor).offset().top;
                    }
                    if(prev != undefined){
                         prev_floor = prev.replace('navfloat','floor');
                         floor_top_prev = $("#"+prev_floor).offset().top;
                    }
                }
                if(l == true){
                    if(now != undefined){
                        if(prev != undefined && scrolltop <= floor_top_prev-30){
                            $("#"+now).find("a").removeClass("now");
                            $("#"+now).prev("li").find('a').addClass("now");
                            $("#"+now_nav).find("a").removeClass("now");
                            $("#"+now_nav).prev("li").find('a').addClass("now");

                            $("#"+now_nav).find("a").removeClass("now");

                $("#"+f).siblings().find('a').removeClass("now");

$(document).ready(function(){
    //var catepath_node = $('#floor_1 .classify_books_detail .classify_title  ').find('a:first');
    var catepath_node = $('.classify_con .classify_books .classify_books_detail .classify_title').find('a:first');
    var one_catepath_reg = /^\d{2}.00.00.00.00.00/;
    var two_catepath_reg = /^58.\d{2}.00.00.00.00/;
    var l ='8fa14cdd754f91cc6554c9e71929cce7'
    $.getJSON('api/get_json.php?type=categoryCrumbs&l='+l,function(e){
        for(var a in e){
            if(a=='errorCode') break;
            $(catepath_node).each(function(ind,val){
                var catepath_val = catepath_node.eq(ind).attr('href');
                if(catepath_val.indexOf(a) >= 0 && catepath_val.indexOf(e[a]['cat_path']) >= 0 && (one_catepath_reg.test(e[a]['cat_path']) || two_catepath_reg.test(e[a]['cat_path']))){
                    catepath_node.eq(ind).attr('href',e[a]['link_url']);
                }
            });
        }
    });
});

    var setTo = null;
    function showghotsearch(){
        clearTimeout(setTo);

    }
    function hidehotsearch(){
        setTo = setTimeout(function(){
          document.getElementById("hot_search_content").style.display="none";
        },100)                        
    }
